NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICES
I, Rajalakshmi Surraj, (daughter of Padmanabhan), aged 41 years, residing at New No. 42, “Vishal Villa”,
5th Main Road, Nanganallur, Chennai-600 061, wish to state that, I have married Shri.L. Surraj Srinivasan,
(son of Thiru Lakshminarayanan) on 11th September 2013 which was duly registered before Marriage Registrar,
S.R.O. Virugambakkam, Chennai-600 092, on 18th September 2013 (M.I. No. 2787/13 dated 18th September 2013).
At the time of my marriage with Shri.Surraj Srinivasan, he had a girl child named ISHVARYA, born on 14th December
2001 (Birth Certificate Reg. No. 1533/2001/3, dated 18th December 2001) for his first wife Mrs. LAKSHMI KRISHNAN.
Mrs. Lakshmi Krishnan died on 19th November 2005 (Death Certificate No. 89/2005/03, dated 23rd November 2005).
By virtue of my marriage with Shri. SURRAJ SRINIVASAN, I have become the Step Mother of ISHVARYA. S.
This public notice is being issued by me, whole heartedly, on my own willing without any prejudice/coersion.

Chennai,
10th August 2015.

P. RAJALAKSHMI SURRAJ.
(Step Mother.)

K. ILAYARAJA a male child born to Mr. P. KARUPPAIYA on 3rd June 1983 residing at No. 495, Ambedkar Nagar,
Theppampatti, Andipatti Taluk, Theni, has been living as a female after an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery
by Dr. S.A.K. Meeran, M.B.B.S., M.S.,(Gen) F.I.C.S., By this I, may be treated as a Female and shall henceforth be
known as K. SWATHI.

Theni,
12th August 2015.

K. ILAYARAJA.

Raja, aged 42, male who is mentally retarded son of (late) K.V. Venkataraman and Tmt. G.V. Muthulakshmi
Venkataraman, born on 9th November 1972 residing at No. 602, Edayarpalayam, Piruvu, Kuniyamuthur, Coimbatore641 008, shall henceforth be known as K.V. RAJA SAMUNDEESWARAN.

Coimbatore,
13th August 2015.

G.V. MUTHULAKSHMI VENKATARAMAN,
